<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выручка.html>вы́ручка</a> (9155)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выручить.html>вы́ручить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výručitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выручка.html>вы́ручка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výručka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выручка.html>вы́ручки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выручка.html>вы́ручки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выручка.html>вы́ручек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gain; proceeds, receipts, takings; earnings
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дневной.html>дневна́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выручка.html>вы́ручка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dnevnája <b>výručka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">daily receipts; the day's receipts</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>rescue, assistance, aid, relief, help
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>прийти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выручка.html>вы́ручку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prijtí na <b>výručku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to come to the rescue</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***вырывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вырывать.html>вырыва́ть</a> (9452)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырыть.html>вы́рыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výrytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырывать.html>вырыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyryvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырыть.html>вы́рыть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dig out, to dig up, to unearth, to exhume</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-рыва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырывать.html>вырыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyryvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырвать.html>вы́рвать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pull out</li>
<li>to tear out</li>
<li>to snatch out <i>(from hands)</i></li>
<li>to pull up <i>(a plant)</i></li>
<li>to eradicate, to extirpate, to root out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to extort, to wring, to wrest</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вырываться.html>вырыва́ться</a> (6318)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырывать.html>вырыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vyryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырываться.html>вырыва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyryvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырваться.html>вы́рваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to break away, to break loose, to escape</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to escape (words, sound, moan, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырывать.html>вырыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vyryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыть.html>рыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садить.html>сади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to set down, to put ashore, to disembark, to land, to put off, to drop off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высадить.html>вы́садить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:десант.html>деса́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výsaditʹ</b> desánt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to land troops; make a landing</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высадить.html>вы́садить</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:судно.html>су́дна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výsaditʹ</b> kovó-libo s súdna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put smb ashore</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smash, to break in, to break open</li>
<li>to transplant, to bed out</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высаживать.html>выса́живавший</a> (25377)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***высаживать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высаживать.html>выса́живать</a> (25377)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высадить.html>вы́садить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výsaditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высаживать.html>выса́живать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vysáživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высадить.html>вы́садить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to set down, to put ashore, to disembark, to land, to put off, to drop off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">высадживать <a href = vnd.unilang:десант.html>деса́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vysadživatʹ desánt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to land troops; make a landing</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высаживать.html>выса́живать</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:судно.html>су́дна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vysáživatʹ</b> kovó-libo s súdna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put smb ashore</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smash, to break in, to break open</li>
<li>to transplant, to bed out</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высадок.html>вы́садка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výsadka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высаживаться.html>выса́живаться</a> (26657)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высаживать.html>выса́живать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vysáživatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высаживаться.html>выса́живаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vysáživatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высадиться.html>вы́садиться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to alight, to dismount <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">from on horseback or from a carriage</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to disembark, to land <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">from a ship</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to get off <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">from a tram or from a train</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высаживать.html>выса́живать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vysáživatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́да</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svobóda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высвободить.html>вы́свободить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výsvoboditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высвобождать.html>высвобожда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to free <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to let out <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to disengage <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to disentangle <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to release, to make available
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высвободить.html>вы́свободить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:средство.html>сре́дства</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:ресурс.html>ресу́рсы</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výsvoboditʹ</b> srédstva (resúrsy)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>release</b> funds (resources)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высвободить.html>вы́свободить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дополнительный.html>дополни́тельные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:средство.html>сре́дства</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výsvoboditʹ</b> dopolnítelʹnyje srédstva (dlja)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>make</b> additional funding <b>available</b> (for)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***высвободиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высвободиться.html>вы́свободиться</a> (19106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высвободить.html>вы́свободить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výsvoboditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высвободиться.html>вы́свободиться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výsvoboditʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высвобождаться.html>высвобожда́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get free from <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высвободиться.html>вы́свободиться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> чьи́х-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výsvoboditʹsja</b> iz čʹíx-libo ruk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get free from someone's grasp</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to get free from someone's hands</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be vacant, to be free
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высвободиться.html>вы́свободилось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výsvobodilosʹ</b> pomeščénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the room became vacant</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высвободить.html>вы́свободить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výsvoboditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высвобождаемый.html>высвобожда́емый</a> (25516)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высвобождать.html>высвобожда́ть</a> (25516)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высвободить.html>вы́свободить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výsvoboditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высвобождать.html>высвобожда́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vysvoboždátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высвободить.html>вы́свободить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to free <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to let out <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to disengage <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to disentangle <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to release, to make available
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высвобождать.html>высвобожда́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:средство.html>сре́дства</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:ресурс.html>ресу́рсы</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vysvoboždátʹ</b> srédstva (resúrsy)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>release</b> funds (resources)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высвобождать.html>высвобожда́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дополнительный.html>дополни́тельные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:средство.html>сре́дства</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vysvoboždátʹ</b> dopolnítelʹnyje srédstva (dlja)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>make</b> additional funding <b>available</b> (for)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высвобождаться.html>высвобожда́ться</a> (29029)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высвобождать.html>высвобожда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vysvoboždátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высвобождаться.html>высвобожда́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vysvoboždátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высвободиться.html>вы́свободиться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get free from <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высвобождаться.html>высвобожда́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> чьи́х-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vysvoboždátʹsja</b> iz čʹíx-libo ruk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get free from someone's grasp</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to get free from someone's hands</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be vacant, to be free
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высвобождаться.html>высвобожда́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:помещение.html>помеще́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vysvoboždálosʹ</b> pomeščénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the room was vacant</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высвобождать.html>высвобожда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vysvoboždátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***высекать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высекать.html>высека́ть</a> (24672)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́сек-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výsek-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высекать.html>высека́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vysekátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высечь.html>вы́сечь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hew, to carve, to sculpt, to cut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высекать.html>высека́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:надпись.html>на́дпись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надгробный.html>надгро́бном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>ка́мне</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vysekátʹ</b> nádpisʹ na nadgróbnom kámne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">carve the inscription on the gravestone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скульптор.html>ску́льптор</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:высекать.html>высека́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мрамор.html>мра́мора</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:статуя.html>ста́тую</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Skúlʹptor <b>vysekájet</b> iz mrámora státuju.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The sculptor <b>is carving</b> the statue out of marble.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:высекать.html>высека́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vysekátʹ</b> ogónʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strike fire (from a flint)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
